                <div n="32" type="adhyāya">

                    <milestone facs="dscn3040 fol 064.jpg lower" n="65r4" unit="folio"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.1"> athātaḥ svabhāvavipratipattiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.3-4"> svabhāvaprasiddhānāṃ śarīraikadeśānām anyathātvaṃ
                        maraṇāya | tad yathā śuklānāṃ kṛṣṇatvaṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ śuklatvaṃ | sthirāṇām
                        mṛdutvaṃ | calānām acalatvam acalā<pb facs="dscn3041 fol 065.jpg upper"
                            n="65v"/><lb n="1"/>nāñ calatvaṃ | pṛthūnāṃ saṃkṣiptatvaṃ saṃkṣiptānāṃ
                        pṛthutvaṃ | dīrghāṇāṃ hrasvatvaṃ ca hrasvānāṃ dīrghatā | apatanadharmmiṇāṃ
                        patanam akasmāc chaityoṣṇasneharaukṣyaprastambhavaivarṇṇyāni apasarppaṇa<g
                            ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><lb n="2"/>m aṅgānāṃ svebhyaḥ sthānebhyaḥ
                        śarīraikadeśānām
                        avasraṃsotkṣiptabhrā<cb/>ntapatitavimuktanirggamātigamagurulaghutvāni
                        pravālavarṇṇavyaṅgaprādurbbhāvo vākasmāt sirāṇāṃ <lb n="3"/>ca darśana
                        lalāṭe nāsāvaṃśe vā piṭakotpattir udakotpattir nne<cb/>trarogam
                        vināsrupravṛttir lalāṭe vā prabhātakāle svedapravṛttiḥ |
                        gomayacūrṇṇaprakāśasya rajaso da<lb n="4"/>rśanam uttamāṅge līyanam vā
                        kapotakaṅkagṛddhraprabhṛtīnāṃ mūtra<cb/>purīṣapravṛddhir abhuñjanānāṃ
                        stanamūlahṛdayorassu ca śūlotpattayaḥ | madhye śūnatvam anteṣu pa<g
                            ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><lb n="5"/>rimlāyitvaṃ | viparyayo vā
                        naṣṭahīnavikalavihṛtasvaraṃ vā vivarṇṇapuṣpaprādurbbhāvo vā
                        dantanakhaśarīreṣu puṣpadarśanaṃ yasya cāpsu kaphaśakṛdretāṃsi nimajjanti
                        yasya <pb facs="dscn3041 fol 065.jpg lower" n="66r"/><lb n="1"/>ca
                        dṛṣṭimaṇḍale bhinnavikṛtāni rūpāṇy ālocyante snehābhyaktakeśāṅga iva yo
                        bhāti yaś ca durbbalo bhaktadveṣātisārābhyām pīḍyate | kāsamānaś ca
                        tṛṣṇātibhūtaḥ kṣīṇaś cha<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><lb n="2"
                        />rddibhaktadeśayuktaḥ saphenarudhirodvāmī hatasvaraḥ śūlābhi<cb/>hataś ca
                        manuṣyaśūnakaracaraṇo nnadveṣī srastapiṇḍakāṃsapāṇipādaḥ | yaś ca pūrvāhṇe
                            bhu<lb n="3"/>ktam aparāhṇe ścharddayaty avidagdhaṃ sāryate vā
                        jvarakāsābhibhūtaḥ <cb/>sa śvāsān mriyate | vastavad vilapamāno bhūmau
                        patati srastamuṣkaḥ stabdhaśepo bhagnagrīvaḥ praṇa<lb n="4"/>ṣṭamehaś ca
                        manuṣyaḥ prāgviśuṣyamāṇahṛdaya ārddraśarīraḥ | <cb/>yaś ca loṣṭaṃ
                        loṣṭenābhihanti | kāṣṭham vā kāṣṭhena tṛṇāni vā cchinnanti | adharoṣṭham vā
                        daśati utta<lb n="5"/>roṣṭham vā leḍhi | āluñcati karṇṇau keśām̐ś ca |
                            devadvijaguru<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/>suhṛdvaidyān vā vidveṣṭi yasya
                        ca vakrānuvakragā grahā garhitasthānagatāḥ | janmaṛkṣam vāsyolkāśa<lb n="6"
                        />nibhyām abhihanyate | rātrau vā
                        gṛhadvāraśayanāśanayānavāhanamaṇiratnopakaraṇagarhitalakṣaṇanimittaprādurbbhāvo
                        veti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5">
                        <abbr type="suspension">bha</abbr><ex cert="medium">vanti cātra</ex> ||
                        <caesura/>
                         cikitsyamānaḥ samyak tu vikāro <pb facs="dscn3042 fol 066.jpg upper"
                            n="66v"/><lb n="1"/>yo bhivarddhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣīṇabala<pc> </pc>māṃsasya lakṣaṇan tadgatāyuṣaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.6"> nivarttate mahāvyādhiḥ sahasā yasya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na cāhāraphalaṃ yasya dṛśyate sa vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.7"> etāni riṣṭarūpāṇi<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/>
                        <lb n="2"/>samyag budhyeta yo bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyāsādhyaparīkṣañ ca sa rājñaḥ sa<cb/>mmato bhaved iti || 31 || ❈ || </l>

                </div>

                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">

                    <milestone facs="dscn3042 fol 066.jpg upper" n="66r2" unit="folio"/>

                    <!--166r, line 2, column 2-->

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.1"> athāto vāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.3"> upadravais tu ye juṣṭā-<lb n="3"/>vyādhayo yānty
                        avāryatāṃ | rasāyanair vvinā vatsa tāṃ śṛṇv ekamanā <cb n="2"/>mama || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.4"> vātavyādhiḥ pramehaś ca kuṣṭhānyatha bhagandaraṃ |
                        arśośmarī mūḍhagarbho bhavaty udaram aṣṭamam <lb n="4"/>|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.5"> aṣṭāv ete mahāntaḥ syūr vvyādhayo dustarāḥ sadā |
                            prāṇamāṃsakṣa<cb n="2"/>yaḥ śophas tṛṣṇā ccharddir jvaras tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.6"> atīsāraś ca mūrcchā ca
                        <caesura/>
                         hikkāśvāsas tathaiva ca | etair upa<lb n="5"/>dravair jjuṣṭān sarvvān etān
                        vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.7"> śūnaṃ suptatvacam bhagnaṅ ka<cb n="2"/>mpādhmānanipīḍitaṃ
                        | rujārttam antañ ca naram vātavyādhir vvināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.8"> yathoktopadravāvi<lb n="6"/>ṣṭam atiprasrutam eva ca |
                        piṭakāpīḍitaṃ gāḍhaṃ prameho hanti mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.9"> prabhinnaṃ prasrutāṅgañ ca raktanetraṃ hatasvaraṃ |
                        pañcakarmmaguṇātītaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ hanti hi kuṣṭhi<pb facs="dscn3042 fol 066.jpg
                            lower" n="67r"/><lb n="1"/>naṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.11"> vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi krimayaḥ śukram eva ca | bhagandarāt
                        prasravanti sa naśyati bhagandarī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.10">
                        <!--the manuscript switches the vulgate 's 10 and 11, as well as 13 and 14-->
                            tṛṣṇarocakaśūlārtta<lb n="2"/>m atiprasrutaśoṇitaṃ |
                        śophātīsārasaṃyuktaṃ durnāmā kṣapayen na<cb n="2"/>raṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.12"> praśūnanābhivṛṣaṇaṃ vaddhamūtrarujāturaṃ | aśmarī
                        kṣapayaty āśu sikatāśarkkarānvitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.14"> pā<lb n="3"/>rśvabhaṅgānnavidveṣaḥ śophātīsārapīḍitam |
                        vivarjayed udariṇa<cb n="2"/>m virikto yo 'bhipūryate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.13"> yonīsamvaraṇaṃ saṅgaḥ kukṣo makkallasaṃjñitaḥ | hanyuḥ
                        striyaṃ mūḍhaga-<lb n="4"/>rvbhe yathoktāś cāpy upadravāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.15"> visaṃjñas tām yate yas tu śete nipati-<cb n="2"/>to
                        yathā | śītārddito 'ntaruṣṇaś ca
                        <caesura/>
                         jvareṇa mriyate naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.16"> yo hṛṣṭaromā raktākṣo hṛdi saṃghātaśūla<lb n="5"/>vān |
                        vaktreṇa cocchvasiti taṃ jvaro hanti mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.17"> hikkāśvāsa samā<cb n="2"/>yuktaṃ mūḍham vibhrāntalocanaṃ
                        | santatocchvāsinaṃ kṣīṇaṃ naraṃ kṣapayate jvaraḥ || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.19"> śvāsaśūlapipāsārtaṃ-<lb n="7"/>kṣīṇañ jvaranipīḍitaṃ |
                        viśeṣeṇa naraṃ vṛddham atīsāro vināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.20"> śuklākṣamannadveṣṭāram ūrddhaśvāsanipīḍitam | kṛcchreṇa
                        vahu mehantaṃ yakṣmā hantīha mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.21"> śvāsaśūlapipā<pb facs="dscn3043 fol 067.jpg upper"
                            n="67v"/><lb n="1"/>sānnavidveṣo granthimūḍhatā | jāyate durvvalatvaṃ ca
                        gulmino maraṇāya vai|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.22"> ādhmānaṃ vaddhaniṣyandaṃ ccharddihikkātṛṣānvitam |
                        rujāśvāsasamāyuktaṃ vidradhir nnāśayet naraṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.23"> pāṇḍudantanakho <lb n="2"/>yastu pāṇḍunetraś ca mānavaḥ
                        | pāṇḍusaṃghātadarśī ca pāṇḍurogī vina<cb/>śyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.24"> lohitañ charddayed yas tu vahuśo lohitekṣaṇaḥ | lohito
                        ṅgāradarśī ca mriyate raktapaittikaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.25">
                        <lb n="3"/>avāco pi savāco 'pi kṣīṇamānsavalo naraḥ | jāgarūko <unclear

                        ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.3"> kecid ācāryā vruvate | <lb n="6"/>dravyam pradhānam
                        kasmāt vyavasthitatvāt | iha khalu dravyam vyavasthitanna rasādayaḥ | yathā
                            <unclear>ye</unclear> phale rasādayas te pakve na bhavanti || nityatvāc
                        ca nityaṃ hi dravyamanityaṃ hi guṇāḥ | yathā ka<pb facs="dscn3056 fol
                            080.jpg lower" n="81r"/><lb n="1"/>lkādi pravibhāgās tad eva
                        sampannarasagandhaṃ vyāpannarasagandhavān bhavatīti | svajātivyavasthānāc ca
                        yathā pārthivaṃ dravyam anyabhāvan na gacchati | evaṃ śoṣāṇi | pañcendri<lb
                            n="2"/>yagrahaṇāc ca | pañcaindriyair gṛhyate draṣṭavyanna
                        rasādaya<cb/>ḥ | āśrayatvāc ca dravyam āśritārasā iti | ārambha sāmarthyāc
                        ca dravyāśrita ārambhaḥ || yathā vidārigandhā<lb n="3"/>dim
                        āhṛtyāva<unclear/>dya vipaced ity evam ādiṣu na rasādiṣ ā<g
                            ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><cb/>rambhaḥ | śāstraprāmāṇyāc ca śāstraṃ
                        <unclear/>ha | dvividhan dravyaṃ sthāvarañjañgam<unclear/>ti |
                        kramāpekṣikatvāc ca rasā<lb n="4"/>dīnāṃ rasādayo hi dravyakramam apekṣante
                        yathā taruṇe ta<cb/>ruṇāḥ | saṃpūrṇa sampūrṇā iti | ekadeśasādhyatvāc ca
                        dravyāṇām ekadeśenāpi vyādhayaḥ sādhyante | yathā<lb n="5"/>
                        mahāvṛkṣakṣīreṇeti | tasmād dravyam pradhānan rasādaya<cb/>ḥ kasmāt
                        niravayavatvāt dravyasya | dravyalakṣaṇan tu kriyāguṇasamavāyaḥ kriyādravye
                        vidyate | guṇāḥ sa<lb n="6"/>mavāyakāraṇañ ceti ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.4"> nety āhur anye rasās tu pradhānan kasmāt āgamāt āgamo hi
                        śāstram ity ucyate | <pb facs="dscn3057 fol 081.jpg" n="81v"/><lb n="1"
                        />śāstre rasā adhikṛtā yathā rasāyatta āhāra iti | upadeśāc ca | upadiśyate
                        hi | yathā madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaṃ śamayanti | <lb n="2"/> ato rasāḥ
                        pradhānaṃ | anumāc ca | rasato hy anumīyate dra<cb/>vyaṃ | yathā madhuram
                        iti || ṛṣivacanāc ca | ṛṣivacano vedaḥ | yathā kiñcidījyārtham
                        madhuramāhared iti<lb n="3"/> | tasmāt rasāḥ pradhānaṃ | raseṣu tu
                        guṇasaṃjñā rasalakṣaṇa<cb/>m atro padekṣyāmaḥ | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.5"> nety āhur anye vīryam pradhānam iti | kasmāt prādhānyāt |
                        ihatvauṣadhakarmmāṇi vīrya prādhā<lb n="4"/>nyaṃ na bhavanti | tad yathā |
                        urddhabhāgodhobhāgobhayabhāgasaṃ<cb/>śamanaṃ
                        sāṅgrāhikadīpanalekhanavṛṃhaṇarasāyanavājīkaraṇaś ca
                            yathuharavilayanadāraṇamarddana<lb n="5"/>prāṇaghnaviṣapraśamanāni vīrya
                        prādhānyena bhavanti | tantu<cb/> vīryaṃ dvividhaṃ | uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ
                        cāgniṣomīyatvāj jagataḥ | kecid aṣṭavidham āhuḥ | uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ snigdhaṃ
                        rūkṣam vi<lb n="6"/> ṣadam piccilam mṛdus tīkṣṇañ ceti | etāni khalu vīryāṇi
                        svabhāvaguṇotkarṣād rasam abhibhūyātmakarmma kurvvanti | yathā tāvad
                        vṛhatyañ ca mūlaṅ kaṣāya tiktaṃ vātaṃ śamayaty uṣṇavīrya<pb
                            facs="dscn3057fol081_bottom.jpg" n="82r"/><lb n="1"/>tvāt | kaṭukā
                        pippalīpittaṃ śamayati | mṛduśītavīryatvāt | tiktā kākamācī pittaṃ
                        varddhayaty uṣṇavīryatvāt | kaṭukaṃ mūlaṃ śleṣmāṇaṃ varddhayati
                        snigdhavīryatvāt | amlaṃ kapitthaṃ śleṣmāṇaṃ <lb n="2"/><unclear/>ti
                        rukṣavīryatvāt || <unclear>bha</unclear> || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.6"> ye rasā vātaśamanā bhavanti <cb/> yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         rukṣalāghavaśaity āni na te hanyuḥ samīraṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.7"> ye rasāḥ pittaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu<g
                            ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><lb n="3"/>vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         taikṣṇyauṣṇyalaghutā caiva na te talkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.8"> ye rasāḥ śleṣma<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><cb/>śamanā
                        bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehagauravaśaity ānu na te tatkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.9"> tasmād vīryaṃ pradhānam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.10">
                        <lb n="4"/>nety āhur anye vipākaḥ pradhānam iti | kasmāt samyaṅ mithyā
                            vipa<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><cb/>kvatvāt | iha hi dravyāṇyapaha tāni
                        samyaṅ mithyā cāvipakvāni guṇan doṣam vā janayaṃti | tatrāhur anye prati
                            ra<lb n="5"/> sampāka iti | vipākaḥ kecit trividham icchanti | madhuram
                        amlam kaṭuka<cb/>ñceti | tat tu na samyak | bhūtaguṇādāgamāc cāmlo vipāko
                        nāsti | pittaṃ hi vidagdham amlatām upaity āgneyatvāt | <lb n="6"/> yad evaṃ
                        lavaṇo 'pyanyaḥ pāke bhaviṣyati | śleṣmā hi vidagdho lavaṇatām upaiti |
                        tamādasiddhānta eṣaḥ | pratirasam amlāmlasyaivaṃ sarvvaṣām iti dṛṣṭāntañ
                        codāharanti | yathā śāliyava<pb facs="dscn3058 fol 082.jpg upper"/><lb n="1"
                        />mudgādayaḥ prakīrṇāḥ svabhāvam uttarakāle pi na parity ajanti tadvat iti |
                        kecit punar avalavanto valavatāṃ vaśamāyānt it evam avasthitaḥ pāka iti |
                        āgame svāha | dvividha eva pāko madhuraḥ kaṭukaś ca <lb n="2"/> | tayor
                        madhurākhyo guruḥ kaṭukākhyo laghur iti | tatra
                        pṛthivyaptejovā<cb/>yvākāśānāṃ dvaividhyam bhavati | guṇasādharmyāngurutā |
                        laghutā ca pṛthivyā yo gurvyaḥ | śeṣāṇi laghūni tasmād dvivi<lb n="3"/>dha
                        eva pāko bhavati || bha ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.11"> dravyeṣu pacyamāneṣu yeṣv amvupṛthi<g
                            ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><cb/>vīguṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivarttante 'dhikās tatra pāko madhura ucyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.12"> tejonilākāśaguṇāḥ pacyamāneṣu yeṣu tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         niva<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><lb n="4"/>rttante 'dhikās tatra pākaḥ
                        kaṭuka ucyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.13"> pṛthak tvavādināmeṣeva vā<cb/>dinām vādasaṃgrahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturṇṇām api sāmagryam icchantyatra vipaścitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.14"> tad dravyam ātmanā kiñcit kiñcid vīryeṇa <lb n="5"/>
                        sevitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kiñcid rasavipākābhyān doṣaṃ hanti karoti vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.15"> pāko nā<cb/>sti vinā vīryād vīryan nāsti vinā rasāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         raso nāsti vinā dravyād dravyaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ smṛtaṃ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.16"> janman tu dravyara<lb n="6"/>sayor anyonyāpekṣikaṃ
                        smṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anyonyāpekṣikaṃ janma yathā syād dehadehinoḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.17"> vīryasaṃjñā guṇā ye 'ṣṭau te 'pi dravyāśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         raseṣu na bhavantyete nirguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.18">
                        <pb facs="dscn3058 fol 082.jpg lower" n="83r"/><lb n="1"/>dravye dravye ca
                        yasmāddhi vipacyante na ṣaḍ rasāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śreṣṭhaṃ dravyamato jñeyaṃ śeṣā bhāvās tadāśrayāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.19"> amīmāṃsyānyacintyāni prasiddhāni svabhāvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āgamenopayojyāni bheṣajāni vica<lb n="2"/>kṣaṇaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.20"> pratyakṣalakṣaṇaphalās prasiddhāś ca svabhāvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         oṣadhīn <cb/>hetubhir vvidvān na parīkṣet kathañcana || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.21"> sahastreṇāpi hetūnān nāmvaṣṭhādir virecayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt tiṣṭhed vima<lb n="3"/>timānāgameśa tu hetuṣu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.21.1">
                        <unclear/>yā svabhāvavijñānaṃ vā raśaṃ yu<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"
                        /><cb/>ktasenikaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āturopakramam miśraṃ bhūmijñānan tathaiva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.21.2">dravyasaṃgrahaṇañ caiva tathā śamanaśodhanaṃ <lb n="4"

                        <caesura/>

                <div n="42" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 42, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <milestone facs="dscn3060 fol 084.jpg lower" n="85r3" unit="folio"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.1"> athāto rasaviśeṣavi<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><cb n="2"
                        />jñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.2"> </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.3"> ākāśapavanadahanatoyabhūmiṣu yathāsaṅkhyam
                        ekottaraparivṛddhāḥ || śa <lb n="4"/> bdasparśarūparasagandhāḥ || tasmād
                        āpyo rasaḥ parasparānupraveśā<cb n="2"/>c ca sarvveṣāṃ sānnidhyam asti
                        utkarṣāt tu grahaṇaṃ | sa khalvāpyo rasaḥ śeṣabhūtasaṃsarggādvidagdhaḥ
                        ṣaḍvidho <lb n="5"/>bhavati | tad yathā | madhuro 'mlo lavaṇaḥ kaṭukastiktaḥ
                        kaṣāya iti | tatrodakavāhulyātmadhuraḥ | toyāgnivāhulyādamlaḥ
                        bhūmyagnivāhulyāl lavaṇaḥ vāyvākāśa<lb n="6"/>vāhulyāttiktaḥ |
                        vāyvagnivāhulyātkaṭukaḥ pṛthivyanilavāhulyātkaṣāya i<cb n="2"/>ti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.4"> tatra madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaghnāḥ | madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.502">mādhuryam annaṅgatamāṃsasaṃjñām vidagdhasaṃjñāṃ gatam amlabhāvaṃ |
                        <caesura/> kiñcid vidagdhaṃ bhṛśatodaśūlam vi<pb facs="dscn3100 fol 122.jpg upper" n="122v"/><lb n="1"/>ṣṭabdham ānaddhaniruddhavātaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.503">udgāraśuddhāvapi bhakṣakāṃkṣā na jāyate hṛdgurutā ca yasya |
                        <caesura/> rasāvaśeṣeṇa tu saprasekaṃ caturtham etan pravadanty ajīrṇṇaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.504">mūrcchā pralāpo vamathuḥ<lb n="2"/>praseko jvaro 'tisāraḥ sadanam bhramaś ca || śirorujā pṛṣṭhaka<cb/>ṭigrahaś ca
                        <caesura/> tṛṣṇāvipāko 'tha vijṛmbhikā ca || upadravā bhavanty ete maraṇam vāpy ajīrṇṇataḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.505">tatrāme <lb n="3"/>laṃghanaṅ kāryam vidagdhe vamanaṃ hitaṃ ||
                        <caesura/> viṣṭabdhe svedanaṃ śastaṃ<cb/> rasaśeṣe śayīta ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.506">vāmayed āśu tan tasmād uṣṇena lavaṇāmvunā ||
                        <caesura/> kāryan cānaśanan tāvad yāvan na pra<lb n="4"/>kṛtim vrajet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.507">laghukāyamanaś cainaṃ laghvannaiḥ samupācaret ||<cb/>
                        <caesura/>
                         yāvan na prakṛtisthaḥ syād doṣataḥ ghrāṇatas tathā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.508">hitāhitopasaṃyuktam anna<pc> </pc><unclear reason="corrections to anusvaras">saṃśamanaṃ</unclear> smṛtaṃ ||
                        <caesura/> vahu<lb n="5"/> stokam akāle vā taṃ jñeyam viṣamāśanaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.509">sājīrṇṇe bhujyate ya<cb/>s tu tad adhyaśanam ucyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tadvad enan nihanty āśu vahūn vyādhīn karoti ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.510">annam vidagdhaṃ hi narasya<lb n="6"/>śīghraṃ śītāmvunā vai paripākam eti |
                        <caesura/> taddhyasya śaity ena nihanti pittam ākledibhāvāc ca na yānty adhastāt ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.511">vidahyate yasya tu bhuktamātraṃ <pb facs="dscn3100 fol 122.jpg lower" n="123r"/><lb n="1"/>dahyanti hṛtkoṣṭhagalām̐ś ca yasya |
                        <caesura/> drākṣāsitāṃ mākṣikasaṃprayuktā līḍhvābhayām vai sasukhaṃ labheta ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.512">bhaved ajīrṇṇaṃ prati yasya śaṅkā snigdhasya jantor vvalino 'nnakāle |
                        <caesura/> prātaḥ saśu<lb n="2"/>ṇṭhīm abhayām aśaṅko bhuñjīta samprāśya hitaṃ
                        hitārthī ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.513">svalpaṃ<cb/> yadā doṣavivandhamāmaṃ līnan na tejaḥ patham āvṛṇoti |
                        <caesura/> bhavanty ajīrṇṇe 'pi tadā vubhukṣā sā ma<lb n="3"/>ndavṛddhim viṣavan
                        nihanti ||<unclear extent="1" unit="syllable"/></l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.514">ata ūrddhvam pravakṣyāmi<cb/> guṇānāṅ karmmavistaraṃ |
                        <caesura/> karmmabhis tv anumīyante nānā dravyāśrayā guṇāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.519cd">daśādyāḥ karmmataḥ proktā<lb n="4"/>s teṣāṅ
                        karmmaviśeṣaṇaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.520ab">daśaivādyām pravakṣyāmi dravādīs tām̐<cb/>ś chṛṇuśva
                        me ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.515">śītaḥ prahlādanastambhī mūrcchātṛṭsvedadāhajit ||1||
                        <caesura/> uṣṇastad viparītaḥ syāt pāca<lb n="5"/>naś ca viśeṣataḥ ||2||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.516">sneho mārddavakṛt snigdho valavarṇṇa<cb/>karas tathā ||3||
                        <caesura/> rūkṣas tad viparītaḥ syād viśeṣāt stambhanaḥ smṛtaḥ ||4||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.517">picchilo jīvanaśle<lb n="6"/>ṣī sandhāno vṛṃhaṇas tathā ||5||
                        <caesura/> viṣado viparīto 'sya bhedī śodhanaropaṇaḥ ||6||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.518">dāhapākakaras tīkṣṇaḥ śrāvaṇo mṛdur anyathā ||8||
                        <caesura/> sāndropalepaḥ kaphakṛ<pb facs="dscn3101 fol 123.jpg upper" n="123v"/><lb
                            n="1"/>d guruḥ prīṇanavṛṃhaṇaḥ ||10||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.519ab">laghus tad viparītaḥ syāl lekhano ropaṇas tathā ||11||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.520cd">dravaḥ prakledanaḥ sāndraḥ śuṣkaḥ syād dvandvakārakaḥ ||13||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.521">ślakṣṇaḥ picchilavaj jñeyaḥ ka<lb n="2"/>rkkaśo viṣado yathā ||15||
                    	<caesura/>sukhānuvarttī sūkṣmañ ca sugandhī<cb/>rocano mataḥ ||16||</l>

            	<l xml:id="SS.1.46.522">durggandho viparīto sya prakāśau cāpy ubhāv api ||17||
                    	<caesura/>saro 'nulomanaḥ<lb n="3"/> prokto mando yātrākaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||19||</l>
            	
            	<l xml:id="SS.1.46.523"> vyavāyī deham akhilaṃ<cb/> vyāpya pākāya kalpate ||20||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.525">guṇā viṃśatir ity ete karmmataḥ parikīrttitāḥ ||<unclear unit="syllable"/></l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.526">ata ūrddham pravakṣyāmi āhāragatiniścayaṃ |
                        <caesura/> pañcabhūtātmake de<cb/>he āhāraḥ pākabhautikaḥ ||
                        <caesura/> vipakvaḥ pañcadhā samyag guṇām̐s tān abhivarddhayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.527">avidagdhaṃ kaphaṃ pittam vidagdhaḥ pavanam punaḥ ||
                        <caesura/> samyag vipakṣo niḥsāra āhāraḥ<cb/> parivṛṃhayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.528">viṇmūtram āhāramalaḥ sāraḥ prāgīrito rasaḥ ||
                        <caesura/> sa tu vyānena vikṣiptaḥ sarvvān dhā<lb n="6"/>tūn visarppati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.529">kapha pitta malaḥ kheṣu svedaḥ syān nakharoma ca ||
                        <caesura/> netraviṭ tvakṣu ca sneho dhātūnāṃ kramaśo malāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.530">divā vivuddhahṛdaye jāgrataḥ puṇḍarīkavat ||
                        <caesura/> anupakli<pb facs="dscn3101 fol 123.jpg lower" n="124r"/><lb n="1"/>nna
                        dhātvannam ajīrṇṇepi hitaṃ niśi |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.531">hṛdayaṃ līyate rātrau prasuptasya viśeṣataḥ ||
                        <caesura/> samupaklinnadhātvannam ajīrṇṇe tvahitaṃ divā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.532">imam vidhiṃ yo 'numatam mahāmuner mmaharṣimu<lb n="2"/>khyasya paṭhet tu yatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/> sa bhūmipāloya vidhātum auṣadham mahā<cb/>tmanāñ cārhati vaidyasattama iti
                        || o ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.533"><add place="inline">dravyajñānaṃ rasajñānam vasanañ ca virecanaṃ |
                            <caesura/> dravadravya<lb n="3"/>parijñānam annapānena ṣaṭ smṛtaḥ || o ||</add></l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.534"><add place="inline">sūtrasthāne purā<cb/> proktañ catvāriṃśat ṣaḍuttaraṃ |
                            <caesura/> adhyāyāḥ kāśirājena pūrṇṇaṃ sarvvaṃ savistaraṃ ||</add></l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.trailer">|| iti <lb n="4"/>suśrute śalyatantre sūtrasthānaṃ
                        samāptaṃ || ||</l>

                    <milestone facs="dscn3101 fol 123.jpg lower" n="124r4" unit="folio"/>

                </div>


            </div>
            <!-- end of Sūtrasthāna -->
	</div>

        </body>

    </text>
